const metricsCards = [
  { label: "Total Searches (30d)", value: "12,847", trend: "+18%", up: true, icon: Search, color: "text-[#0057A8]", bg: "bg-[#0057A8]/10" },
  { label: "Avg Response Time", value: "42ms", trend: "-12%", up: true, icon: Activity, color: "text-emerald-600", bg: "bg-emerald-50" },
  { label: "Codes Retrieved", value: "284,930", trend: "+23%", up: true, icon: Database, color: "text-[#F28C28]", bg: "bg-[#F28C28]/10" },
  { label: "Compliance Score", value: "97.4%", trend: "+0.8%", up: true, icon: ShieldCheck, color: "text-purple-600", bg: "bg-purple-50" },
];

const container = { hidden: { opacity: 0 }, visible: { opacity: 1, transition: { staggerChildren: 0.1 } } };
const itemAnim = { hidden: { opacity: 0, y: 20 }, visible: { opacity: 1, y: 0, transition: { duration: 0.4 } } };

export function Analytics() {
  return (
    <motion.div
      variants={container}
      initial="hidden"
      animate="visible"
      className="p-6 space-y-6 min-h-full"
    >
      <motion.div variants={itemAnim} className="grid grid-cols-2 xl:grid-cols-4 gap-5">
        {metricsCards.map((m) => (
          <motion.div
            key={m.label}
            whileHover={{ y: -4 }}
            className="bg-white rounded-2xl p-5 border border-border/50 shadow-sm hover:shadow-lg hover:shadow-primary/5 transition-all"
          >
            <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-4">
              <div className={`w-11 h-11 ${m.bg} rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center`}>
                <m.icon className={`w-5 h-5 ${m.color}`} />
              </div>
              <div className={`flex items-center gap-1 text-xs font-bold px-2 py-1 rounded-lg ${m.up ? "bg-emerald-50 text-emerald-600" : "bg-red-50 text-red-600"}`}>
                {m.up ? <TrendingUp className="w-3 h-3" /> : <TrendingDown className="w-3 h-3" />}
                {m.trend}
              </div>
            </div>
            <p className="text-2xl font-black text-foreground tracking-tight">{m.value}</p>
            <p className="text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground mt-1">{m.label}</p>
          </motion.div>
        ))}
      </motion.div>

      <motion.div variants={itemAnim} className="bg-white rounded-2xl p-6 border border-border/50 shadow-sm">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-6">
          <div>
            <h2 className="text-base font-black text-foreground">Search Volume by Code Type</h2>
            <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground font-medium mt-0.5">8-week trend across all code categories</p>
          </div>
          <div className="flex gap-4 text-xs font-bold">
            {["ICD-10-CM", "CPT", "HCPCS"].map((t, i) => (
              <div key={t} className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
                <div className="w-2.5 h-2.5 rounded-full" style={{ background: COLORS[i] }} />
                <span className="text-muted-foreground">{t}</span>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
        <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height={240}>
          <AreaChart data={weeklyTrend} margin={{ top: 5, right: 5, left: -30, bottom: 0 }}>
            <defs>
              {["icd", "cpt", "hcpcs"].map((key, i) => (
                <linearGradient key={key} id={`grad-${key}`} x1="0" y1="0" x2="0" y2="1">
                  <stop offset="5%" stopColor={COLORS[i]} stopOpacity={0.1} />
                  <stop offset="95%" stopColor={COLORS[i]} stopOpacity={0} />
                </linearGradient>
              ))}
            </defs>
            <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" stroke="#f1f5f9" />
            <XAxis dataKey="week" tick={{ fontSize: 10, fontWeight: 600, fill: "#94a3b8" }} axisLine={false} tickLine={false} />
            <YAxis tick={{ fontSize: 10, fill: "#94a3b8" }} axisLine={false} tickLine={false} />
            <Tooltip contentStyle={{ borderRadius: "12px", border: "1px solid #e2e8f0", fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 600 }} />
            <Area type="monotone" dataKey="icd" stroke={COLORS[0]} strokeWidth={2} fill={`url(#grad-icd)`} />
            <Area type="monotone" dataKey="cpt" stroke={COLORS[1]} strokeWidth={2} fill={`url(#grad-cpt)`} />
            <Area type="monotone" dataKey="hcpcs" stroke={COLORS[2]} strokeWidth={2} fill={`url(#grad-hcpcs)`} />
          </AreaChart>
        </ResponsiveContainer>
      </motion.div>

      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 xl:grid-cols-5 gap-6">
        <motion.div variants={itemAnim} className="xl:col-span-3 bg-white rounded-2xl p-6 border border-border/50 shadow-sm">
          <h2 className="text-base font-black text-foreground mb-1">CPT Category Breakdown</h2>
          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground font-medium mb-5">Distribution by medical specialty</p>
          <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height={220}>
            <BarChart data={categoryDistribution} layout="vertical" margin={{ top: 0, right: 20, left: 10, bottom: 0 }}>
              <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" stroke="#f1f5f9" horizontal={false} />
              <XAxis type="number" tick={{ fontSize: 10, fill: "#94a3b8" }} axisLine={false} tickLine={false} />
              <YAxis dataKey="category" type="category" tick={{ fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 600, fill: "#64748b" }} axisLine={false} tickLine={false} width={90} />
              <Tooltip
                formatter={(v) => [Number(v).toLocaleString(), "Codes"]}
                contentStyle={{ borderRadius: "12px", border: "1px solid #e2e8f0", fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 600 }}
              />
              <Bar dataKey="value" radius={[0, 8, 8, 0]}>
                {categoryDistribution.map((_, i) => <Cell key={i} fill={COLORS[i % COLORS.length]} />)}
              </Bar>
            </BarChart>
          </ResponsiveContainer>
        </motion.div>

        <motion.div variants={itemAnim} className="xl:col-span-2 bg-white rounded-2xl p-6 border border-border/50 shadow-sm">
          <h2 className="text-base font-black text-foreground mb-1">Compliance Metrics</h2>
          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground font-medium mb-4">Data quality &amp; accuracy scores</p>
          <div className="space-y-4">
            {complianceData.map((c) => (
              <div key={c.name}>
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-1.5">
                  <span className="text-xs font-bold text-foreground">{c.name}</span>
                  <span className="text-sm font-black" style={{ color: c.fill }}>{c.value}%</span>
                </div>
                <div className="h-2.5 bg-slate-100 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
                  <motion.div
                    initial={{ width: 0 }}
                    animate={{ width: `${c.value}%` }}
                    transition={{ duration: 1, delay: 0.3, ease: "easeOut" }}
                    className="h-full rounded-full"
                    style={{ background: c.fill }}
                  />
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>

          <div className="mt-6 p-4 bg-emerald-50 rounded-xl border border-emerald-100">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <div className="w-2 h-2 bg-emerald-500 rounded-full animate-pulse" />
              <span className="text-xs font-black text-emerald-700">Overall Compliance: 97.4%</span>
            </div>
            <p className="text-xs text-emerald-600 font-medium mt-1">All metrics within CMS thresholds</p>
          </div>
        </motion.div>
      </div>

      <motion.div variants={itemAnim} className="bg-white rounded-2xl p-6 border border-border/50 shadow-sm">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-5">
          <div>
            <h2 className="text-base font-black text-foreground">Peak Usage Hours</h2>
            <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground font-medium mt-0.5">Query volume by hour of day (24h)</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height={160}>
          <BarChart data={hourlyUsage} margin={{ top: 5, right: 5, left: -30, bottom: 0 }}>
            <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" stroke="#f1f5f9" />
            <XAxis dataKey="hour" tick={{ fontSize: 10, fontWeight: 600, fill: "#94a3b8" }} axisLine={false} tickLine={false} tickFormatter={(v) => `${v}:00`} />
            <YAxis tick={{ fontSize: 10, fill: "#94a3b8" }} axisLine={false} tickLine={false} />
            <Tooltip
              labelFormatter={(l) => `${l}:00 hrs`}
              contentStyle={{ borderRadius: "12px", border: "1px solid #e2e8f0", fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 600 }}
            />
            <Bar dataKey="queries" fill="#0057A8" radius={[6, 6, 0, 0]} />
          </BarChart>
        </ResponsiveContainer>
      </motion.div>
    </motion.div>
  );
}


--- client/src/pages/Favorites.tsx ---
import { useFavorites } from "@/hooks/use-favorites";
import { CodeCard } from "@/components/codes/CodeCard";
import { LoadingState } from "@/components/ui/LoadingState";
import { ErrorState } from "@/components/ui/ErrorState";
import { Bookmark, Search, Star } from "lucide-react";
import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
import { Link } from "wouter";
import { motion } from "framer-motion";

export function Favorites() {
  const { data: favorites, isLoading, isError, refetch } = useFavorites();

  const containerVariants = {
    hidden: { opacity: 0 },
    visible: {
      opacity: 1,
      transition: {
        staggerChildren: 0.1,
        delayChildren: 0.2,
      },
    },
  };

  const itemVariants = {
    hidden: { opacity: 0, y: 20 },
    visible: {
      opacity: 1,
      y: 0,
      transition: { duration: 0.4, ease: "easeOut" },
    },
  };

  return (
    <div className="p-6 max-w-5xl min-h-full relative">
      <div className="absolute -top-20 -right-20 w-40 h-40 bg-accent/5 rounded-full blur-3xl" />
      <div className="absolute -bottom-20 -left-20 w-40 h-40 bg-primary/5 rounded-full blur-3xl" />
      
      <motion.div 
        initial={{ opacity: 0, y: -20 }}
        animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
        transition={{ duration: 0.5 }}
        className="relative flex items-center gap-4 mb-12"
      >
        <motion.div 
          animate={{ rotate: [0, 10, -10, 0] }}
          transition={{ repeat: Infinity, duration: 4 }}
          className="w-14 h-14 rounded-2xl bg-gradient-to-br from-accent to-secondary/50 flex items-center justify-center shadow-lg shadow-accent/30"
        >
          <Bookmark className="w-7 h-7 text-white" />
        </motion.div>
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-4xl font-black text-foreground tracking-tight">Your Workspace</h1>
          <p className="text-lg text-muted-foreground font-medium">Curated medical codes for rapid access</p>
        </div>
      </motion.div>

      {isLoading ? (
        <LoadingState message="Loading your workspace..." />
      ) : isError ? (
        <ErrorState onRetry={() => refetch()} />
      ) : favorites?.length === 0 ? (
        <motion.div 
          initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95 }}
          animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1 }}
          transition={{ duration: 0.5 }}
          className="relative text-center py-32 bg-white/50 backdrop-blur rounded-3xl border border-border/50 shadow-2xl shadow-primary/5 group overflow-hidden"
        >
          <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-br from-accent/5 via-transparent to-primary/5 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-1000" />
          <motion.div 
            animate={{ y: [0, -10, 0] }}
            transition={{ repeat: Infinity, duration: 3 }}
            className="relative"
          >
            <Star className="w-20 h-20 text-muted-foreground/20 mx-auto mb-6" />
          </motion.div>
          <h3 className="text-2xl font-black text-foreground mb-3 relative">Start Building Your Workspace</h3>
          <p className="text-muted-foreground mb-8 max-w-sm mx-auto text-lg relative">
            Save frequently-used diagnosis and procedure codes for instant access and clinical reference.
          </p>
          <Link href="/">
            <motion.div whileHover={{ scale: 1.05 }} whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}>
              <Button size="lg" className="rounded-full shadow-xl shadow-primary/30 gap-2 font-bold text-base">
                <Search className="w-5 h-5" /> Explore Medical Records
              </Button>
            </motion.div>
          </Link>
        </motion.div>
      ) : (
        <motion.div 
          variants={containerVariants}
          initial="hidden"
          animate="visible"
          className="relative grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-6"
        >
          {favorites?.map((fav, idx) => (
            <motion.div key={fav.id} variants={itemVariants}>
              <CodeCard 
                code={{
                  type: fav.codeType,
                  code: fav.code,
                  description: fav.description
                }}
                onClick={() => {}}
              />
            </motion.div>
          ))}
        </motion.div>
      )}

      <motion.div 
        initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
        animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
        transition={{ delay: 0.8 }}
        className="mt-16 text-center text-sm text-muted-foreground"
      >
        <p className="font-semibold tracking-widest uppercase">
          {favorites?.length || 0} Code{favorites?.length !== 1 ? "s" : ""} Saved
        </p>
      </motion.div>
    </div>
  );
}


--- client/src/pages/AnesthesiaCalculator.tsx ---
import { useState } from "react";
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from "framer-motion";
import { Calculator, MapPin, Clock, DollarSign, Info, ChevronDown } from "lucide-react";
import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/card";
import { Badge } from "@/components/ui/badge";
import { useQuery } from "@tanstack/react-query";

interface Locality {
  id: number;
  Contractor: string;
  Locality: string;
  "Locality Name": string;
  "2026 Work GPCI": string;
  "2026 PE GPCI": string;
  "2026 MP GPCI": string;
  non_qualifying_cf: string;
  qualifying_cf: string;
}

interface CalcResult {
  locality: string;
  localityName: string;
  contractor: string;
  workGpci: number;
  peGpci: number;
  mpGpci: number;
  nonQualifyingCf: number;
  qualifyingCf: number;
  usedCf: number;
  baseUnits: number;
  timeUnits: number;
  modifierUnits: number;
  totalUnits: number;
  payment: number;
}

export function AnesthesiaCalculator() {
  const [selectedLocality, setSelectedLocality] = useState("");
  const [baseUnits, setBaseUnits] = useState<number>(0);
  const [timeMinutes, setTimeMinutes] = useState<number>(0);
  const [modifierUnits, setModifierUnits] = useState<number>(0);
  const [useQualifying, setUseQualifying] = useState(false);
  const [result, setResult] = useState<CalcResult | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState("");

  const { data: localities } = useQuery({
    queryKey: ["/api/anesthesia/localities"],
    queryFn: async () => {
      const res = await fetch("/api/anesthesia/localities", { credentials: "include" });
      const data = await res.json();
      return data.filter((l: Locality) => l["Locality Name"]) as Locality[];
    }
  });

  const timeUnits = parseFloat((timeMinutes / 15).toFixed(2));
  const totalUnits = baseUnits + timeUnits + modifierUnits;

  const calculate = async () => {
    if (!selectedLocality) { setError("Please select a locality"); return; }
    if (baseUnits <= 0) { setError("Please enter base units"); return; }
    setError("");
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetch(
        `/api/anesthesia/calculate?locality=${encodeURIComponent(selectedLocality)}&baseUnits=${baseUnits}&timeUnits=${timeUnits}&modifierUnits=${modifierUnits}&qualifying=${useQualifying}`,
        { credentials: "include" }
      );
      const data = await res.json();
      setResult(data);
    } catch {
      setError("Calculation failed. Please try again.");
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="p-8 max-w-5xl mx-auto space-y-8">
      <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-4 mb-2">
          <div className="w-12 h-12 bg-primary/10 rounded-2xl flex items-center justify-center">
            <Calculator className="w-6 h-6 text-primary" />
          </div>
          <div>
            <h1 className="text-3xl font-black text-foreground tracking-tight">Anesthesia Calculator</h1>
            <p className="text-muted-foreground font-medium">CY 2026 Locality-Adjusted Conversion Factors</p>
          </div>
          <Badge className="ml-auto bg-green-100 text-green-700 border-green-200 font-black">
            National CF: $20.4975
          </Badge>
        </div>
      </motion.div>

      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-6">
        {/* Input Panel */}
        <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, x: -20 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }} transition={{ delay: 0.1 }}>
          <Card className="border-2 h-full">
            <CardHeader>
              <CardTitle className="text-lg font-black">Enter Details</CardTitle>
            </CardHeader>
            <CardContent className="space-y-6">

              {/* Locality */}
              <div className="space-y-2">
                <label className="text-sm font-black text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider flex items-center gap-2">
                  <MapPin className="w-4 h-4" /> Locality
                </label>
                <div className="relative">
                  <select
                    className="w-full h-12 px-4 rounded-xl border-2 border-border bg-white text-sm font-medium focus:border-primary outline-none appearance-none cursor-pointer"
                    value={selectedLocality}
                    onChange={(e) => setSelectedLocality(e.target.value)}
                  >
                    <option value="">Select locality...</option>
                    {localities?.map((l) => (
                      <option key={l.id} value={l.Locality?.trim()}>
                        {l["Locality Name"]} (CF: ${Number(l.non_qualifying_cf).toFixed(2)})
                      </option>
                    ))}
                  </select>
                  <ChevronDown className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground pointer-events-none" />
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* Base Units */}
              <div className="space-y-2">
                <label className="text-sm font-black text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider">
                  Base Units (from CPT code)
                </label>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                  <button onClick={() => setBaseUnits(Math.max(0, baseUnits - 1))}
                    className="w-10 h-10 rounded-xl border-2 border-border font-bold text-lg hover:border-primary transition-colors">-</button>
                  <input
                    type="number"
                    min="0"
                    className="flex-1 h-10 text-center border-2 border-border rounded-xl font-black text-xl focus:border-primary outline-none"
                    value={baseUnits}
                    onChange={(e) => setBaseUnits(Number(e.target.value))}
                  />
                  <button onClick={() => setBaseUnits(baseUnits + 1)}
                    className="w-10 h-10 rounded-xl border-2 border-border font-bold text-lg hover:border-primary transition-colors">+</button>
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* Time */}
              <div className="space-y-2">
                <label className="text-sm font-black text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider flex items-center gap-2">
                  <Clock className="w-4 h-4" /> Time (minutes) = {timeUnits.toFixed(2)} units
                </label>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                  <button onClick={() => setTimeMinutes(Math.max(0, timeMinutes - 15))}
                    className="w-10 h-10 rounded-xl border-2 border-border font-bold text-lg hover:border-primary transition-colors">-</button>
                  <input
                    type="number"
                    min="0"
                    step="15"
                    className="flex-1 h-10 text-center border-2 border-border rounded-xl font-black text-xl focus:border-primary outline-none"
                    value={timeMinutes}
                    onChange={(e) => setTimeMinutes(Number(e.target.value))}
                  />
                  <button onClick={() => setTimeMinutes(timeMinutes + 15)}
                    className="w-10 h-10 rounded-xl border-2 border-border font-bold text-lg hover:border-primary transition-colors">+</button>
                </div>
                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">1 time unit = 15 minutes</p>
              </div>

              {/* Modifier Units */}
              <div className="space-y-2">
                <label className="text-sm font-black text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider">
                  Qualifying Circumstances Units (optional)
                </label>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                  <button onClick={() => setModifierUnits(Math.max(0, modifierUnits - 1))}
                    className="w-10 h-10 rounded-xl border-2 border-border font-bold text-lg hover:border-primary transition-colors">-</button>
                  <input
                    type="number"
                    min="0"
                    className="flex-1 h-10 text-center border-2 border-border rounded-xl font-black text-xl focus:border-primary outline-none"
                    value={modifierUnits}
                    onChange={(e) => setModifierUnits(Number(e.target.value))}
                  />
                  <button onClick={() => setModifierUnits(modifierUnits + 1)}
                    className="w-10 h-10 rounded-xl border-2 border-border font-bold text-lg hover:border-primary transition-colors">+</button>
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* APM Type */}
              <div className="space-y-2">
                <label className="text-sm font-black text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider">Provider Type</label>
                <div className="flex gap-2">
                  {[
                    { label: "Non-Qualifying APM", value: false },
                    { label: "Qualifying APM", value: true }
                  ].map((opt) => (
                    <button
                      key={String(opt.value)}
                      onClick={() => setUseQualifying(opt.value)}
                      className={`flex-1 py-2.5 rounded-xl text-xs font-black border-2 transition-all ${
                        useQualifying === opt.value
                          ? "bg-primary text-white border-primary"
                          : "bg-white text-muted-foreground border-border hover:border-primary/50"
                      }`}
                    >
                      {opt.label}
                    </button>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* Total Units Preview */}
              <div className="bg-slate-50 rounded-2xl p-4 border border-border/50">
                <p className="text-xs font-black text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider mb-2">Total Units Preview</p>
                <p className="text-2xl font-black text-foreground">
                  {baseUnits} + {timeUnits.toFixed(2)} + {modifierUnits} = <span className="text-primary">{totalUnits.toFixed(2)}</span>
                </p>
                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">Base + Time + Qualifying</p>
              </div>

              {error && <p className="text-sm text-red-500 font-medium">{error}</p>}

              <button
                onClick={calculate}
                disabled={loading}
                className="w-full h-12 bg-primary text-white rounded-xl font-black text-base hover:bg-primary/90 transition-colors disabled:opacity-50 flex items-center justify-center gap-2"
              >
                {loading ? (
                  <div className="w-5 h-5 border-2 border-white/30 border-t-white rounded-full animate-spin" />
                ) : (
                  <>
                    <Calculator className="w-5 h-5" />
                    Calculate Payment
                  </>
                )}
              </button>
            </CardContent>
          </Card>
        </motion.div>

        {/* Result Panel */}
        <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, x: 20 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }} transition={{ delay: 0.2 }}>
          <AnimatePresence mode="wait">
            {result ? (
              <motion.div
                key="result"
                initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95 }}
                animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1 }}
                exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
                className="space-y-4 h-full"
              >
                {/* Payment Result */}
                <Card className="border-2 border-primary bg-primary/5">
                  <CardContent className="p-8 text-center">
                    <p className="text-sm font-black text-primary uppercase tracking-wider mb-2">Medicare Payment</p>
                    <p className="text-6xl font-black text-primary">${result.payment.toFixed(2)}</p>
                    <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-2">
                      {result.totalUnits.toFixed(2)} units × ${result.usedCf.toFixed(4)} CF
                    </p>
                    <Badge className="mt-3 bg-primary/10 text-primary border-primary/20 font-bold">
                      {result.localityName}
                    </Badge>
                  </CardContent>
                </Card>

                {/* Locality Details */}
                <Card className="border-2">
                  <CardContent className="p-6 space-y-4">
                    <h3 className="font-black text-sm uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground">Locality Details</h3>
                    <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
                      {[
                        { label: "Work GPCI", value: result.workGpci.toFixed(3) },
                        { label: "PE GPCI", value: result.peGpci.toFixed(3) },
                        { label: "MP GPCI", value: result.mpGpci.toFixed(3) },
                        { label: "Used CF", value: `$${result.usedCf.toFixed(4)}` },
                        { label: "Non-Qualifying CF", value: `$${result.nonQualifyingCf.toFixed(2)}` },
                        { label: "Qualifying CF", value: `$${result.qualifyingCf.toFixed(2)}` },
                      ].map((item) => (
                        <div key={item.label} className="bg-slate-50 rounded-xl p-3">
                          <p className="text-xs font-black text-muted-foreground uppercase">{item.label}</p>
                          <p className="text-lg font-black text-foreground">{item.value}</p>
                        </div>
                      ))}
                    </div>
                  </CardContent>
                </Card>

                {/* Unit Breakdown */}
                <Card className="border-2">
                  <CardContent className="p-6">
                    <h3 className="font-black text-sm uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground mb-4">Unit Breakdown</h3>
                    <div className="space-y-2">
                      {[
                        { label: "Base Units", value: result.baseUnits, color: "bg-blue-500" },
                        { label: "Time Units", value: result.timeUnits, color: "bg-green-500" },
                        { label: "Qualifying Units", value: result.modifierUnits, color: "bg-orange-500" },
                      ].map((item) => (
                        <div key={item.label} className="flex items-center justify-between">
                          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                            <div className={`w-3 h-3 rounded-full ${item.color}`} />
                            <span className="text-sm font-medium">{item.label}</span>
                          </div>
                          <span className="font-black">{item.value.toFixed(2)}</span>
                        </div>
                      ))}
                      <div className="pt-2 border-t border-border flex items-center justify-between">
                        <span className="text-sm font-black">Total Units</span>
                        <span className="text-xl font-black text-primary">{result.totalUnits.toFixed(2)}</span>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </CardContent>
                </Card>

                <div className="p-4 bg-slate-50 rounded-2xl border border-border/50 flex items-start gap-3">
                  <Info className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground flex-shrink-0 mt-0.5" />
                  <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                    Payment = Total Units × Locality-Adjusted CF. Actual Medicare payment may vary. Does not include CRNA or medically directed rates.
                  </p>
                </div>
              </motion.div>
            ) : (
              <motion.div
                initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
                animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
                className="h-full flex flex-col items-center justify-center text-muted-foreground p-12 text-center border-2 border-dashed border-border/50 rounded-3xl min-h-[400px]"
              >
                <div className="w-24 h-24 bg-primary/5 rounded-[2rem] flex items-center justify-center mb-6 border border-primary/10">
                  <DollarSign className="w-12 h-12 text-primary/30" />
                </div>
                <h2 className="text-2xl font-black text-foreground mb-2">Calculate Payment</h2>
                <p className="text-sm font-medium max-w-xs">
                  Select a locality, enter base units and time, then click Calculate
                </p>
              </motion.div>
            )}
          </AnimatePresence>
        </motion.div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}


--- client/src/pages/Search.tsx ---

import { useState, useEffect } from "react";
import { useDebounce } from "use-debounce";
import { Search as SearchIcon, Filter, Stethoscope } from "lucide-react";
import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";
import { ScrollArea } from "@/components/ui/scroll-area";
import { Tabs, TabsList, TabsTrigger } from "@/components/ui/tabs";
import { useSearchCodes } from "@/hooks/use-codes";
import { CodeCard } from "@/components/codes/CodeCard";
import { CodeDetails } from "@/components/codes/CodeDetails";
import { LoadingState } from "@/components/ui/LoadingState";
import { ErrorState } from "@/components/ui/ErrorState";
import { MedicalCode } from "shared/schema";
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from "framer-motion";
import { Card, CardContent, CardHeader, CardTitle } from "@/components/ui/card";

const CODE_TYPES = ["All", "ICD-10-CM", "CPT", "HCPCS"];

export function Search() {
  const [searchTerm, setSearchTerm] = useState("");
  const [debouncedSearch] = useDebounce(searchTerm, 300);
  const [selectedType, setSelectedType] = useState("All");
  const [selectedCode, setSelectedCode] = useState<MedicalCode | null>(null);

  const { data: codes, isLoading, isError, refetch } = useSearchCodes(debouncedSearch, selectedType);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (codes && codes.length > 0 && !selectedCode) {
      setSelectedCode(codes[0]);
    }
  }, [codes, selectedCode]);

  return (
    <div className="flex gap-8 p-8">
      {/* Left Column */}
      <div className="w-[480px] flex-shrink-0 space-y-8">
        {/* Search & Filter */}
        <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }} animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }} transition={{ delay: 0.1 }}>
          <Card className="glass-morphism-card">
            <CardHeader>
              <CardTitle className="text-2xl font-bold">Search Records</CardTitle>
              <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground font-medium">114,000+ codes indexed</p>
            </CardHeader>
            <CardContent className="space-y-4">
              <div className="relative group">
                <SearchIcon className="absolute left-4 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-5 h-5 text-muted-foreground group-focus-within:text-primary transition-colors" />
                <Input
                  placeholder="Diagnosis or procedure..."
                  className="pl-12 h-14 rounded-2xl border-2 border-border/50 focus-visible:ring-primary focus-visible:border-primary text-base shadow-inner bg-secondary/5 font-medium transition-all"
                  value={searchTerm}
                  onChange={(e) => setSearchTerm(e.target.value)}
                />
              </div>
              <Tabs value={selectedType} onValueChange={setSelectedType} className="w-full">
                <TabsList className="w-full flex bg-muted/50 p-1.5 rounded-2xl gap-1">
                  {CODE_TYPES.map(type => (
                    <TabsTrigger
                      key={type}
                      value={type}
                      className="flex-1 rounded-xl text-xs font-bold data-[state=active]:bg-primary data-[state=active]:text-white data-[state=active]:shadow-lg transition-all py-2.5"
                    >
                      {type}
                    </TabsTrigger>
                  ))}
                </TabsList>
              </Tabs>
            </CardContent>
          </Card>
        </motion.div>

        {/* Code List */}
        <ScrollArea className="h-[calc(100vh-26rem)] -mx-2 px-2">
          <div className="space-y-4 pb-8">
            {isLoading ? (
              <LoadingState message="Scanning database..." />
            ) : isError ? (
              <ErrorState title="Search Failed" message="Could not retrieve codes." onRetry={() => refetch()} />
            ) : codes?.length === 0 ? (
              <div className="text-center p-12 text-muted-foreground bg-muted/20 rounded-3xl border-2 border-dashed border-border/50">
                <Filter className="w-16 h-16 mx-auto mb-4 opacity-10" />
                <p className="font-bold">No matches found</p>
                <p className="text-xs mt-1">Try broadening your search terms</p>
              </div>
            ) : (
              <AnimatePresence mode="popLayout">
                {codes?.map((code, i) => (
                  <CodeCard
                    key={`${code.type}-${code.code}-${i}`}
                    code={code}
                    isSelected={selectedCode?.code === code.code}
                    onClick={() => setSelectedCode(code)}
                  />
                ))}
              </AnimatePresence>
            )}
          </div>
        </ScrollArea>
      </div>

      {/* Right Column (Details) */}
      <div className="flex-1 space-y-8">
        <AnimatePresence mode="wait">
          {selectedCode ? (
            <motion.div
              key={`${selectedCode.type}-${selectedCode.code}`}
              initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.98, y: 10 }}
              animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1, y: 0 }}
              exit={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.98, y: -10 }}
              transition={{ duration: 0.3, ease: "easeOut" }}
              className="h-full glass-morphism-card overflow-hidden"
            >
              <CodeDetails codeItem={selectedCode} />
            </motion.div>
          ) : (
            <motion.div
              initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
              className="h-full flex flex-col items-center justify-center text-muted-foreground p-12 text-center glass-morphism-card"
            >
              <div className="w-32 h-32 bg-primary/5 rounded-[2.5rem] flex items-center justify-center mb-8 shadow-xl border border-primary/10 animate-bounce-slow">
                <Stethoscope className="w-16 h-16 text-primary" />
              </div>
              <h2 className="text-3xl font-black text-foreground mb-4 tracking-tight">Precision Medical Intelligence</h2>
              <p className="max-w-md text-lg font-medium text-muted-foreground leading-relaxed">
                Select a code from the directory to unlock deep clinical insights, cross-walk mapping, and real-time CMS compliance data.
              </p>
            </motion.div>
          )}
        </AnimatePresence>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-6">
            <div>
              <h2 className="text-base font-black text-foreground">Weekly Search Activity</h2>
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground font-medium mt-0.5">Queries processed this week</p>
            </div>
            <span className="text-xs font-bold bg-[#0057A8]/10 text-[#0057A8] px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl">Last 7 days</span>

            </AreaChart>

              />
            </PieChart>
          </ResponsiveContainer>
          <div className="space-y-2 mt-3">
            {pieData.map((entry, idx) => (
              <div key={entry.name} className="flex items-center justify-between text-xs">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <div className="w-2.5 h-2.5 rounded-full" style={{ background: COLORS[idx] }} />
                  <span className="font-semibold text-muted-foreground">{entry.name}</span>
                </div>
                <span className="font-black text-foreground">{entry.value.toLocaleString()}</span>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </motion.div>
      </div>

      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 xl:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
        <motion.div variants={item} className="xl:col-span-2 bg-white rounded-2xl p-6 border border-border/50 shadow-sm">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-6">
            <div>
              <h2 className="text-base font-black text-foreground">Code Database Breakdown</h2>
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground font-medium mt-0.5">Records per code type</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height={180}>
            <BarChart data={barData} margin={{ top: 5, right: 5, left: -30, bottom: 0 }}>
              <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" stroke="#f1f5f9" />
              <XAxis dataKey="name" tick={{ fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 700, fill: "#94a3b8" }} axisLine={false} tickLine={false} />
              <YAxis tick={{ fontSize: 11, fill: "#94a3b8" }} axisLine={false} tickLine={false} tickFormatter={(v) => `${(v / 1000).toFixed(0)}k`} />
              <Tooltip
                formatter={(value) => [Number(value).toLocaleString(), "Codes"]}
                contentStyle={{ borderRadius: "12px", border: "1px solid #e2e8f0", fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 600 }}
              />
              <Bar dataKey="value" radius={[8, 8, 0, 0]}>
                {barData.map((entry, idx) => <Cell key={idx} fill={entry.fill} />)}
              </Bar>
            </BarChart>
          </ResponsiveContainer>
        </motion.div>

        <motion.div variants={item} className="bg-white rounded-2xl p-6 border border-border/50 shadow-sm">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
            <h2 className="text-base font-black text-foreground">Recent Activity</h2>
            <Link href="/search">
              <span className="text-xs font-bold text-[#0057A8] hover:underline cursor-pointer flex items-center gap-1">
                View all <ArrowRight className="w-3 h-3" />
              </span>
            </Link>
          </div>
          <div className="space-y-3">
            {recentActivity.map((a, i) => (
              <motion.div
                key={i}
                initial={{ opacity: 0, x: 10 }}
                animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
                transition={{ delay: i * 0.1 }}
                className="flex items-center gap-3 p-2 rounded-xl hover:bg-slate-50 transition-colors cursor-pointer group"
              >
                <div className="w-9 h-9 rounded-xl bg-[#0057A8]/10 flex items-center justify-center flex-shrink-0">
                  <span className="text-[9px] font-black text-[#0057A8]">{a.type.split("-")[0]}</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                    <span className="text-sm font-black text-foreground">{a.code}</span>
                    <span className="text-[9px] font-bold text-white bg-[#0057A8] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full">{a.type}</span>
                  </div>
                  <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate font-medium">{a.desc}</p>
                </div>
                <span className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground font-semibold flex-shrink-0 flex items-center gap-1">
                  <Clock className="w-3 h-3" /> {a.time}
                </span>
              </motion.div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </motion.div>
      </div>

      <motion.div variants={item}>
        <h2 className="text-base font-black text-foreground mb-4">Quick Actions</h2>
        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-4">
          {quickActions.map((action) => (
            <Link key={action.href} href={action.href}>
              <motion.div
                whileHover={{ scale: 1.03, y: -3 }}
                whileTap={{ scale: 0.97 }}
                className="bg-white rounded-2xl p-5 border border-border/50 shadow-sm hover:shadow-lg hover:shadow-primary/5 transition-all cursor-pointer group"
              >
                <div className={`w-12 h-12 ${action.color} rounded-2xl flex items-center justify-center mb-4 group-hover:scale-110 transition-transform`}>
                  <action.icon className="w-6 h-6 text-white" />
                </div>
                <p className="text-sm font-black text-foreground">{action.label}</p>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-1 mt-2 text-[#0057A8] opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity">
                  <span className="text-xs font-bold">Open</span>
                  <ArrowUpRight className="w-3 h-3" />
                </div>
              </motion.div>
            </Link>
          ))}
        </div>
      </motion.div>

      <motion.div
        variants={item}
        className="relative overflow-hidden rounded-2xl p-6 text-white shadow-xl"
        style={{ background: "linear-gradient(135deg, #0057A8 0%, #003d75 60%, #F28C28 130%)" }}
      >
        <div className="absolute -top-10 -right-10 w-40 h-40 bg-white/5 rounded-full blur-2xl" />
        <div className="absolute -bottom-10 -left-5 w-32 h-32 bg-white/5 rounded-full blur-2xl" />
        <div className="relative flex flex-col md:flex-row items-start md:items-center justify-between gap-4">
          <div>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2">
              <Zap className="w-5 h-5 text-[#FFD700]" />
              <span className="text-xs font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-white/70">System Status</span>
            </div>
            <h3 className="text-2xl font-black tracking-tight">All Systems Operational</h3>
            <p className="text-white/60 text-sm font-medium mt-1">
              Database online · 114,240 codes indexed · CMS guidelines synced
            </p>
          </div>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <div className="w-2 h-2 bg-emerald-400 rounded-full animate-pulse" />
            <span className="text-sm font-bold text-white/80">Live &amp; Compliant</span>
          </div>
        </div>
      </motion.div>
    </motion.div>
  );
}


--- client/src/index.css ---
